***наварить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наварить.html>навари́ть</a> (24800)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:варить.html>вари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">varítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наварить.html>навари́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navarítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нава́ривать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cook (some amount of food)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metallurgy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to boil (a quantity of steel) in an open-hearth furnace</li>
<li>to lengthen by welding</li>
<li>to weld on</li>
<li>to profit</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навар.html>нава́р</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">navár</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наваристый.html>нава́ристый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">naváristyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навевать.html>навева́ть</a> (22215)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навеять.html>наве́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">navéjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навевать.html>навева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навеять.html>наве́ять</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to blow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:навевать.html>навева́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:прохлада.html>прохла́ду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">véter <b>navevájet</b> proxládu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wind blows refreshingly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cast <i>(over)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навевать.html>навева́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тоска.html>тоску́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-л</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navevátʹ</b> toskú na kovó-l</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cast a gloom over smb; plunge smb into gloom</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навевать.html>навева́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сон.html>сны</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navevátʹ</b> sny</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to call up dreams; evoke dreams</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***навевающий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навевать.html>навева́ющий</a> (22215)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">навед-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naved-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наведение.html>наведе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navedénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наведение.html>наведе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наведение.html>наведе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наведение.html>наведе́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> induction

<li>aiming, pointing, homing, guidance

<li>establishing, putting

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наведение.html>наведе́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:справка.html>спра́вок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">navedénije správok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">making inquiries</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наведение.html>наведе́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядок.html>поря́дка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">navedénije porjádka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">putting things in order; establishment of order</span></div></dd>

***навернуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навернуть.html>наверну́ть</a> (30886)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вернуть.html>верну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навернуть.html>наверну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navernútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">навёртывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wrap (something) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative, onto something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to screw (something) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative, onto something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навернуть.html>наверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:крышка.html>кры́шку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бутылка.html>буты́лку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navernútʹ</b> krýšku na butýlku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to screw a cover onto a bottle</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to wrap onto,to screw onto</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">наверте́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">navertétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навернуться.html>наверну́ться</a> (24251)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навернуть.html>наверну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">navernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навернуться.html>наверну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navernútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">навёртываться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wind <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative, around something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to screw <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative, onto something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to appear <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of tears in the eyes</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn up, to appear unexpectedly <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">somewhere</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навернуть.html>наверну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">navernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:несомненно.html>несомне́нно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:верный.html>ве́рно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:точно.html>то́чно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:достоверно.html>достове́рно</a>; разг.: стопудово, стопудняк <a href = vnd.unilang:железный.html>желе́зно</a>; устар.: <a href = vnd.unilang:наверное.html>наве́рное</a>, наверняк</li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">верста́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">verstátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наверстать.html>наверста́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naverstátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наверстывать.html>навёрстывать</a></b>)

***навес.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навес.html>наве́с</a> (8105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навесить.html>наве́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">navésitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hang on, suspend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навес.html>наве́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navés</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навес.html>наве́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навес.html>наве́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навес.html>наве́сов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>awning, shed, lean-to <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">an open-sided structure with a roof</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">finance</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> overhang</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lob, lobbed ball</li></ol>

***навесить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навесить.html>наве́сить</a> (18889)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>ве́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vésitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навесить.html>наве́сить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navésitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навешивать.html>наве́шивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hang up, to suspend
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навесить.html>наве́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navésitʹ</b> dverʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hang a door</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навесить.html>наве́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>замок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navésitʹ</b> zamok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fix a padlock; fasten a padlock</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to load <i>(with)</i>, to tax <i>(with)</i>, to charge <i>(with)</i>, to saddle <i>(with)</i>, to lumber <i>(with)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lob
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навесить.html>наве́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мяч.html>мяч</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высоко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голово́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:соперник.html>сопе́рника</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navésitʹ</b> mjač vysoko nad golovój sopérnika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lob the ball high above the opponent's head</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́</a> (6162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_3">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наводить.html>наводи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to direct <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to aim <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to point <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:орудие.html>ору́дие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navestí</b> orúdije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to point a gun</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:след.html>след</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navestí</b> na sled</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put on the trail</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navestí</b> na myslʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to suggest an idea <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to somebody</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cover, to coat, to apply
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лоск.html>лоск</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глянец.html>гля́нец</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navestí</b> losk, <b>navestí</b> gljánec</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to gloss, to glaze, to veneer</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:красота.html>красоту́</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navestí</b> krasotú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to beautify oneself</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядок.html>поря́док</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navestí</b> porjádok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put a place in order, to introduce order, to establish order</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скука.html>ску́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navestí</b> skúku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bore</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:страх.html>страх</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navestí</b> strax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to inspire fear</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:критика.html>кри́тику</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navestí</b> krítiku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to criticize</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:справка.html>спра́вки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navestí</b> správki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to inquire, to make inquiries</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тень.html>тень</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navestí</b> tenʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to complicate matters, to confuse things</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to bring in <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">a quantity</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навешать.html>наве́шавший</a> (27271)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навешать.html>наве́шать</a> (27271)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вешать.html>ве́шать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">véšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навешать.html>наве́шать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navéšatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навешивать.html>наве́шивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to weigh out <i>(a quantity of)</i></li>
<li>to hang up <i>(a number of)</i>, to suspend <i>(a quantity of)</i></li>
<li>to give it <i>(to)</i>, to give the business, to give the works</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навешенный.html>наве́шенный</a> (18889)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навешенный.html>наве́шенный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navéšennyj</span>)

***навешивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навешивать.html>наве́шивать</a> (32286)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навесить.html>наве́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">navésitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навешать.html>наве́шать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">navéšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навешивать.html>наве́шивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navéšivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навесить.html>наве́сить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навешать.html>наве́шать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hang up, to suspend
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навешивать.html>наве́шивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navéšivatʹ</b> dverʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hang a door</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навешивать.html>наве́шивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ярлык.html>ярлыки́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navéšivatʹ</b> jarlykí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to label; tag</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to load <i>(with)</i>, to tax <i>(with)</i>, to charge <i>(with)</i>, to saddle <i>(with)</i>, to lumber <i>(with)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lob</li>
<li>to weigh out <i>(a quantity of)</i>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навешать.html>наве́шать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">navéšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навес.html>наве́с</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">navés</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">навесно́й</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">navesnój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
